Pumping lemma

    It 'L' is an infinite language then there exists some positive integer 'n' such that any 
string W belongs to L, has length >= n, |w| >=n, then w can be divided into three parts, 
w = xyz, satisfy following condition,

i) For each i>0, xy^iz belongs L
ii) |Y|>0
